
Cumulocity IoT Open-Source Repository Overview
==============================================


This Repository generates on a daily basis a table of all open-source repositories for Cumulocity-IoT. It should give a brief overview of all available IoT open-source repositories for Cumulocity IoT including additional content at TechCommunity.

Number of Open-Source Repos: **491**


Table of contents
=================

* [5 Newest Repositories](#5-newest-repositories)
* [Open-Source Repository Overview Table](#open-source-repository-overview-table)
* [Open-Source Repository Detail Lists](#open-source-repository-detail-lists)
	* [All Categories](#all-categories)
	* [Microservices](#microservices)
	* [Widgets](#widgets)
	* [Webapps](#webapps)
	* [Agents](#agents)
	* [Examples](#examples)
	* [Clients](#clients)
	* [Simulators](#simulators)
	* [Documentations](#documentations)
	* [Tutorials](#tutorials)
	* [Extensions](#extensions)
	* [CLIs](#clis)
	* [Others](#others)

### [SoftwareAG/cumulocity-remote-access-cloud-http-proxy](https://github.com/SoftwareAG/cumulocity-remote-access-cloud-http-proxy)


**Description**: A Cumulocity IoT microservice that allows to proxy HTTP requests through the cloud to an HTTP server running on a Cumulocity IoT connected device.

**Owner**: SoftwareAG

### [SoftwareAG/cumulocity-video-widget](https://github.com/SoftwareAG/cumulocity-video-widget)


**Description**: Plays streaming videos from sources such as HLS streams, on-demand videos (such as MP4, MKV, MOV) from URL and embedded YouTube, Vimeo, etc. videos. Please note that links must be HTTPS and Cross-Origin access enabled. This has been developed by Software AG Global Presales team.

### [qvest-digital/KNIME-Cumulocity-Connector](https://github.com/qvest-digital/KNIME-Cumulocity-Connector)


**Description**: The ‚ÄúCumulocity Nodes‚Äù collection of nodes provides functionality to retrieve information about IoT devices, corresponding measurements, alarms and events from a given Cumulocity IoT platform instance. This data, possibly in combination with any other data, can be used to create new events and alarms within KNIME and write them back to Cumulocity in order to trigger the corresponding actions within Cumulocity.
